## About Me
I'm a software developer focused on building scalable web applications, reliable APIs, and delightful developer experiences. I care about clean architecture, observability, and shipping production-ready features.

## What I Do
- Build maintainable frontend and backend systems
- Design scalable APIs and data-driven architectures
- Improve developer experience with tooling and automation
- Mentor and collaborate across design, product, and QA

## Tech Stack

- Backend: Node.js, Express, FastAPI  
- Databases: PostgreSQL, Redis, MongoDB  
- Cloud / DevOps: Docker, Kubernetes, AWS  
- Testing: Jest, Playwright, pytest
